 Anand Bakshi Sahab's name as a lyricist is recorded in golden letters in the history of Indian cinema
 21july 1930 ko rawalpindi (ab pakistan main) main janme anand bakshi ne ek se badhkar ek gane hindi filmon ko die hai
 Famous composers of that era, Laxmikant Pyarelal, Rahul Dev Burman, Kalyanji Anandji, Viju Shah, Roshan, Rajesh Roshan and Anand Bakshi were also among the many favorite writers

 donon filmo ko suraj prakaash bana rahe the

 ' Citing the increase in crimes against minors by women, a parliamentary committee has recommended reducing the teenage age of boys from 18 years to 16 years
 saath hi samiti ne mahilaon ke khilaaf kishoron dwaara kiye jane vaale aparaadhon kii rokthaam ke uddeshy se aavashyak kadam uthaane ke liye gambhir bahes karne kaa suzav bhi diya he
 The Parliamentary Committee on Empowerment of Women, citing data provided by various agencies, has requested the Central Government to reduce the adolescent age of boys from 18 years to 16 years for the crimes committed by them against women
 They can be prosecuted under various laws of the country
 ’ In the report titled 'sexual Abuse and Sex Trafficking and Rehabilitation', the committee said that in 2010, the juveniles committed 22,740 punishable offenses under the Indian Penal Code
 varsh 2011 main yah aankada 10
 Increased 5 percent to 25,125
 report main kaha gaya he ki mahilaon ke khilaaf kishoron dwaara kiye jane vaale aparaadh main lagaataar vruddhi hui he
 In 2010, juveniles were involved in 858 rape cases, 391 abductions of women and 536 molestation cases
 varsh 2011 main balaatkaar ke 1,149 maamalon, mahilaon ke apharan ke 600 maamalon or chhedchhad ke 573 maamalon main kishor lipt the
 The committee also analyzed the profiles of the juveniles caught and found that most of the crimes were committed by juveniles between the ages of 16 and 18 years
 kishor nyaay kanoon, 1986 ke anusaar 16 saal se kam umr ke ladke or 18 saal se kam umr kii ladki ko kishor mana gaya tha

 '' AK Srivastava, the key witness in the 2G spectrum allocation scandal, will testify in the special court on Monday
 shrivastav doorsanchaar vibhaag ke purv varisht adhikari hai
 The statement of AK Srivastava, former Deputy Director General of Department of Telecommunications, will be recorded in the court of Special CBI Judge OP Saini on Monday
 is maamle main shrivastav kii gavaahi kaaphi mahatvapurn he kyonki unhone sibiai ko diye bayaan main kaha tha ki tatkaaleen doorsanchaar mantri e raja ne doorsanchaar vibhaag kii file par note lagayaa tha ki 2ji spectrum license ke liye aavedan sweekaar karne kii tithi ek aktubar 2007 hogi
 According to the charge sheet of the Central Bureau of Investigation, A
 Raja allegedly decided to accept the applications given in the Department of Telecommunications by September 25 as part of a conspiracy to benefit some communications companies
 jaanch beuro ke anusaar, raja unitech wireles (tamilnadu) li or swaan telecom ko laabh pahunchaana chaahate the or isi prakriya main unhone apni marji se aavedan sweekaar karne kii antim taarikh gata di thi
 The Bureau of Investigation claims that during this process, Raja completely ignored various departments including Telecom Regulatory Authority, Law Ministry and Prime Minister's Office
 shrivastav kii gavaahi jaanch beuro ke liye bahut mahatvapurn he
 Srivastava said during the investigation that RK Chandolia, the then personal secretary of Raja, also questioned him on 24 September 2007 about the applications accepted till then
 shrivastav ke anusaar jaise hi unhone bataaya ki unitech samooh kii companiyon ke aavedan 24 sitambar ko hi mil gayi hai, to chandoliya ne unhen nirdesh diya ki agle din se uniphoid acces services license ke liye koi nayaa aavedan sweekaar nahin kiya jaye
 The comments is maamle main raja or chandoliya ke saath hi dramuk saansad kanimoi, purv sanchaar sachiv siddharth behura, swaan telikam ke pramotor shahid osman balava or vinod goyanka tathaa unitech li ke prabandh nideshak sanjay chandra sahit kai abhiyukt hai
 These include senior officials of Reliance ADAG Gautam Doshi, Hari Nair and Surendra Pipara, directors of Kusegaon Fruits and Vegetables Pvt Ltd Asif Balwa, Rajeev Agarwal, filmmaker Karim Morani and Sharad Kumar, managing director of Kalaignar TV
 2ji spectrum aavanton maamle main in 14 abhiyukton ke alaava teen telikam companiyaan swaan telikam pra li, reliance telikam li or unitech wireles (tamilnadu) bhi aaropee hai
 Srivastava's testimony in this case is significant as he said in a statement to the CBI that the then Telecom Minister a Raja had noted on the file of the Department of Telecommunications that the date for accepting the application for 2G spectrum license would be October 1, 2007
 kendriya jaanch beuro ke aarope patr ke anusaar kuch sanchaar companiyon ko laabh pahunchane kii sajeesh ke tahat e raja ne doorsanchaar vibhaag main diye gaye aavednon ko 25 sitambar tak hi sweekaar karne kaa kathith rup se nirnay kiya
 According to the Bureau of Investigation, Raja wanted to benefit Unitech Wireless (tamil Nadu) Ltd and Swan Telecom and in the same process, he voluntarily reduced the last date to accept the application
 jaanch beuro kaa daawa he ki is prakriya ke dauraan raja ne doorsanchaar niamak praadhikaran, kanoon mantralay or pradhanmantri karyaalay sahit vibhinn vibhaagon ko puri tarah nanjarandaaj kiya
 Srivastava's testimony is very important to the Bureau of Investigation
 shrivastav ne jaanch ke dauraan kaha tha ki raja ke tatkaaleen nijee sachiv aarake chandoliya ne 24 sitambar, 2007 ko unase tab tak sweekaar kiye gaye aavednon ke bare main poochtacha bhi kii thi
 According to Srivastava, as soon as he told that the applications of Unitech group companies had been received only on 24 September, Chandolia instructed him that no new application for Unified Access Services license should be accepted from the next day
 tippaniyan Raja and Chandolia are accused in the case along with DMK MP Kanimozhi, former communications secretary Siddharth Behura, Swan Telecom promoters Shahid Usman Balwa and Vinod Goenka and Unitech Ltd managing director Sanjay Chandra
